Atta has been &#8220;named as one of the most influential LGBT people in the UK by the Independent on Sunday and &#8216;one of poetry’s greatest modern voices&#8217; by Gay Times&#8221;, <a href=\"https://www.hachette.co.uk/contributor/dean-atta/\">per Hachette UK</a>. </p>\n<p><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062990292/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0062990292\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"The Black Flamingo\" data-publisher=\"Balzer + Bray\" data-releasedate=\"2020-05-26\" class=\"butter\">The Black Flamingo </a>is a novel in verse that explores identity; the book was recognized as a Stonewall Award winner. For more from Atta, there is also his work, <a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1908906162/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1908906162\" class=\"butter\">I Am Nobody&#8217;s Nigger</a>. <em>The Black Flamingo</em> was <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/2020-queer-audiobooks/\">among the best queer audiobooks in 2020 on Book Riot.</a></p>\n<p>When asked if poetry can change the world, Atta said via <a href=\"https://www.timeout.com/london/lgbt/dean-atta-interview-poetry-can-be-life-changing\">Time Out</a>, &#8220;I believe it can &#8211; whether it&#8217;s one person picking up a poetry book or a video that goes viral on YouTube. Poetry can be life changing.&#8221; </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Light-at-Bottom-World/dp/1368036880/ref=sr_1_1?dchild=1&#38;keywords=london+shah&#38;qid=1595777318&#38;s=books&#38;sr=1-1\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/The-Light-at-the-Bottom-of-the-World-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-441155\" width=\"200\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/The-Light-at-the-Bottom-of-the-World-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg 334w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/The-Light-at-the-Bottom-of-the-World-Book-Cover-201x300.jpg.optimal.jpg 201w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/The-Light-at-the-Bottom-of-the-World-Book-Cover-251x375.jpg.optimal.jpg 251w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/The-Light-at-the-Bottom-of-the-World-Book-Cover-33x50.jpg.optimal.jpg 33w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 334px) 100vw, 334px\" /></a></figure></div>\n<h3>London Shah</h3>\n<p>If you like otherworldly stories, consider reading London Shah&#8217;s dystopian sci-fi writing. According to <a href=\"https://www.londonshah.com/\">Shah&#8217;s website</a>, &#8220;<a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1368036880/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1368036880\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"The Light at the Bottom of the World (Light the Abyss (1))\" data-publisher=\"Little, Brown Books for Young Readers\" data-releasedate=\"2019-10-29\" class=\"butter\">The Light at the Bottom of the World</a> is her debut novel and the first in the Light the Abyss duology.&#8221; The story takes place in an underwater, future world. </p>\n<p>The Light at the Bottom of the World was picked as a Junior Library Guild selection; a &#8220;Best Fiction for Young Adults 2020&#8221; book by the Young Adult Library Services Association; and other selections. It&#8217;s included among <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/best-genre-blending-young-adult-novels/\">10 of the Best Genre Blending Young Adult Novels of 2019 on Book Riot</a>. </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly/dp/1471178773/ref=sr_1_1?dchild=1&#38;keywords=danielle+jawando&#38;qid=1595777403&#38;s=books&#38;sr=1-1\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/And-the-Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-441156\" width=\"200\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/And-the-Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg 326w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/And-the-Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly-Book-Cover-196x300.jpg.optimal.jpg 196w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/And-the-Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly-Book-Cover-245x375.jpg.optimal.jpg 245w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/And-the-Stars-Were-Burning-Brightly-Book-Cover-33x50.jpg.optimal.jpg 33w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 326px) 100vw, 326px\" /></a></figure></div>\n<h3>Danielle Jawando</h3>\n<p>Author Danielle Jawando has <a href=\"https://madeleinemilburn.co.uk/mm-authors/danielle-jawando/\">written for the stage and television</a>, including for the show <em>Coronation Street</em>, a very popular soap opera in the United Kingdom. </p>\n<p><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1471178773/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1471178773\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"And the Stars Were Burning Brightly\" data-publisher=\"Simon &#38; Schuster Childrens Books\" data-releasedate=\"2020-03-01\" class=\"butter\">And The Stars Were Burning Brightly</a> is Jawando&#8217;s debut novel. The story explores the aftermath of a young man&#8217;s suicide and his younger brother&#8217;s journey to find answers. Her book was selected as one of 5 UK YA Books to Read in 2020 in a <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/5-uk-ya-books-to-read-in-2020/\">Book Riot article</a>. </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/1509874054/ref=sr_1_1?dchild=1&#38;keywords=muhammad+khan&#38;qid=1595778075&#38;sr=8-1\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/I-Am-Thunder-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-441157\" width=\"200\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/I-Am-Thunder-Book-Cover.jpg.optimal.jpg 330w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/I-Am-Thunder-Book-Cover-198x300.jpg.optimal.jpg 198w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/I-Am-Thunder-Book-Cover-248x375.jpg.optimal.jpg 248w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/I-Am-Thunder-Book-Cover-33x50.jpg.optimal.jpg 33w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 330px) 100vw, 330px\" /></a></figure></div>\n<h3>Muhammad Khan</h3>\n<p>Not only does author Muhammad Khan write, he&#8217;s an <a href=\"https://www.panmacmillan.com/authors/muhammad-khan/f977c673-fe67-4587-6520-08d5dd18a203\">engineer and teacher</a> too. Books by Khan include <a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" class=\"butter\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1509874054/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1509874054\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-title=\"I Am Thunder [Jan 25, 2018] Khan, Muhammad\" data-publisher=\"Macmillan Children's Books\" data-releasedate=\"2020-09-01\">I Am Thunder</a> and <a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" class=\"butter\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1509874070/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1509874070\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-title=\"Kick the Moon\" data-publisher=\"Macmillan Children's Books\" data-releasedate=\"2021-01-01\">Kick The Moon</a>. According to <a href=\"https://www.panmacmillan.com/authors/muhammad-khan/f977c673-fe67-4587-6520-08d5dd18a203\">Pan MacMillan</a>, &#8220;<em>I Am Thunder </em>was shortlisted for the YA Book Prize, won the Branford Boase First Novel Award, the 2018 Great Reads Award and a number of regional awards.&#8221;  </p>\n<p>In 2018, Book Riot <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/interview-muhammad-khan/\">published an interview with Khan</a>. 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"Donating Books During COVID-19","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=444258","description":"\n<p>With all acknowledgement of my privilege, I must say that the COVID-related cancellation that hit me the hardest was my town library&#8217;s annual book sale. This sale is my Christmas, Super Bowl, and COLUMBUS DIDN&#8217;T DISCOVER AMERICA Day all rolled into one. I eagerly await it each year. And the glory comes in waves. Wave 1 is me going through my library to weed out which books I want to donate to the sale. Why do I currently own four copies of <em>The Lonely Polygamist</em> and three copies of <em>The Boy in the Striped Pajamas</em>? Admittedly, Wave 1 is entirely in service of Wave 2, replacing those donated books…and then some. <br><br>While I always had a special spot in my heart for Wave 2, this global pandemic has made it very clear to me just how important a regular annual cleaning of books is to my mental and physical well-being. Mental because mess and clutter has always caused me psychological angst. And physical because, well, I don&#8217;t want to be crushed by 78 copies of books about polygamy and the Holocaust. <br><br>Since so many annual book sales across the globe were cancelled, I wanted to share some ways in which you can clear out your book clutter (to make more room for impulse quarantine book purchases). These suggestions are contingent on local infection rates and the individual branches. As always, please practice all necessary precautions while donating. Do not donate your items if you or someone in your household are ill. Wear a mask during your donation and be sure to follow social distancing measures.</p>\n<h2>Half-Priced Books</h2>\n<p>Half-Priced Books is currently purchasing used books from the public. Limited hours and restrictions apply. Contact your specific location for more information.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.hpb.com/stuff-we-buy\"> https://www.hpb.com/stuff-we-buy </a></p>\n<h2>Goodwill/Salvation Army</h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.goodwill.org/locator/\">https://www.goodwill.org/locator/</a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://satruck.org/\">https://satruck.org/</a></p>\n<h2>Facebook Marketplace</h2>\n<p>If you&#8217;d like to get a little cash for your books, consider listing them on Facebook Marketplace. Determine the safest and most secure way to exchange the books with the buy so all parties are comfortable.</p>\n<h2>Books for Africa</h2>\n<p>Books for Africa is the largest shipper of donated text and library books to the African continent. </p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.booksforafrica.org/donate/donate-books.html\">https://www.booksforafrica.org/donate/donate-books.html</a></p>\n<h2>Your Local Book Bank</h2>\n<p>You will likely have to call in advance and make an appointment to deliver your donations. Go to your local Book Bank&#8217;s website for more information.</p>\n<h2>Operation Paperback</h2>\n<p>This organization focuses on getting paperback books into the hands of active duty American soldiers. They are accepting donations during COVID and have asked volunteers to take proper precautions</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://operationpaperback.org/\">https://operationpaperback.org/</a></p>\n<h2>Donate to a Teacher</h2>\n<p>Each school and individual teacher will likely have their own policy about accepting donations for their classroom or school library. If you have a teacher friend, reach out to them and ask if they could use any age-appropriate books you might be willing to donate.</p>\n<h2>Little Free Libraries</h2>\n<p>Due to the fact that so many people were stuck in their houses for so long, the cupboards are pretty bare at a lot of local Little Free Libraries. Individual stewards of Little Free Libraries have been called to make their own choices about whether or not they wish for their libraries to remain open during this time. Check out the below map to find one closest to you.</p>\n<p> <a href=\"https://littlefreelibrary.org/ourmap/\">https://littlefreelibrary.org/ourmap/</a> </p>\n<h2>Donate to a Friend</h2>\n<p>My friends and I are currently dropping off books in each other&#8217;s mailboxes. We also have used our local bookstore as a way station. The owner of our local indie is happy to have us drop off books in anticipation of it being picked up. The bonus: we&#8217;re all likely to purchase a book while there!</p>\n<h2>Your Local Library</h2>\n<p>Some public libraries have reopened their acceptance of used books. Please contact your local branch to see if they are accepting donations at this time.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"Comics for People With Anxiety","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=441656","description":"\n<p>Anxiety is bad enough in the best of times—which these clearly are not—and stress about meeting arbitrary reading goals or not having the energy to crack open the newest bestseller sometimes makes reading hard even for a diehard bookworm like me. But even when I&#8217;m not up for my usual reading habits, comics are always there. Being able to pick up a comic and finish it in one or two sittings is a real comfort to me. It&#8217;s a way to escape, even when I don&#8217;t have the energy for more involved reading. Not only that, plenty of comic writers/artists out there have experiences with mental illness of their own. And some of them have brought their love of sequential art together with those experiences to create some incredible comics for people with anxiety. Don&#8217;t believe me? Just take a look. </p>\n<h2>Excellent Comics for People With Anxiety</h2>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/fresh-off-the-vine.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em>Fresh off the Vine</em> by Ariel Slamet Ries</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>A semi-autobiographical webcomic about an eggplant—yes, an eggplant—who&#8217;s very good at pretending to be cooler and calmer than they really are. But just like the rest of us, that cool exterior hides a whole lot of anxieties. </p><p>You can read the mini comic on <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"Ries' website (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://arielries.com/portfolio/fresh-off-the-vine/\" target=\"_blank\">Ries&#8217;s website</a>, whose name you might also recognize as the author of another excellent webcomic, <em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/154930481X/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=154930481X\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Witchy\" data-publisher=\"Oni Press\" data-releasedate=\"2019-09-17\" class=\"butter\">Witchy</a></em>. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1449486061/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1449486061\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/quiet-girl-in-a-noisy-world.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1449486061/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1449486061\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Quiet Girl in a Noisy World: An Introvert's Story\" data-publisher=\"Andrews McMeel Publishing\" data-releasedate=\"2017-11-07\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><em>Quiet Girl in a Noisy World: An Introvert’s Story</em></a> by Debbie Tung </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Introversion and social anxiety amidst a world of extroverts who just don&#8217;t seem to understand. Tung&#8217;s experiences as a self-proclaimed quiet girl are super relatable. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/the-worriers-guide-to-life.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1449477542/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1449477542\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Worrier's Guide to Life 2017 Wall Calendar\" data-publisher=\"Andrews McMeel Publishing\" data-releasedate=\"2016-06-07\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Worrier&#8217;s Guide to Life</a></em> by Gemma Correll</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Gemma Correll is a worrier—bet a lot of you can relate. I know I can. Especially when she&#8217;s drawing random comics and slice-of-life moments about wandering thoughts during yoga, insomnia, hypochondriac tendencies, and befriending the resident animal at social gatherings. Anxiety problems, am I right?</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/the-fire-never-goes-out.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062278274/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0062278274\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"The Fire Never Goes Out: A Memoir in Pictures\" data-publisher=\"HarperTeen\" data-releasedate=\"2020-03-03\" class=\"butter\">The Fire Never Goes Out: A Memoir in Pictures</a> </em>by Noelle Stevenson</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Stevenson&#8217;s graphic memoir draws from her experiences as a young artist and the highs and lows of finding unexpected success at such a young age. Struggles with anxiety and depression feature prominently, and especially as a fellow creative with anxiety, I really connected with the meaning behind the title: the fire never goes out. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/bird-brain-chuck-mullin.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1524854581/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1524854581\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Bird Brain: Comics About Mental Health, Starring Pigeons\" data-publisher=\"Andrews McMeel Publishing\" data-releasedate=\"2019-11-19\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Bird Brain</a></em> by Chuck Mullin</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Mullin&#8217;s reasons for choosing to depict her struggles with anxiety as a pigeon alter-ego—that people dismiss and degrade the formerly domesticated bird in the same way her brain often does to her—is too relatable. And her comics are too!</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/everything-is-beautiful-and-im-not-afraid.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1524852457/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1524852457\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Everything Is Beautiful, and I'm Not Afraid: A Baopu Collection\" data-publisher=\"Andrews McMeel Publishing\" data-releasedate=\"2020-03-03\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Everything is Beautiful and I&#8217;m Not Afraid: a Baopu Collection</a></em> by Yao Xiao</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Yao Xiao explores the particular anxiety of being a queer woman in a family and culture that aren&#8217;t always understanding or accepting of that fact. Beautiful, twisty artwork follows Yao&#8217;s mental journey of self-reflection and acceptance as a young, queer immigrant. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/everyones-a-aliebn-when-ur-a-aliebn-too.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062569023/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0062569023\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Everyone's a Aliebn When Ur a Aliebn Too: A Book\" data-publisher=\"Harper Perennial\" data-releasedate=\"2017-06-27\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Everyone&#8217;s a Aliebn When Ur a Aliebn Too</a></em> by Jomny Sun</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>A little aliebn tries to figure out what exactly it means to be human, but it&#8217;s harder than expected. Especially because everyone they talk to is struggling to figure out their own identity issues. Also: none of them are human. Oops. </p><p>This comic isn&#8217;t explicitly about anxiety, but the worries explored throughout and the care and compassion shown make it a great read for people who know what it&#8217;s like to struggle with worries and self-doubt. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/thin-slices-of-anxiety.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1452145792/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1452145792\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Thin Slices of Anxiety: Observations and Advice to Ease a Worried Mind\" data-publisher=\"Chronicle Books\" data-releasedate=\"2016-04-19\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Thin Slices of Anxiety</a></em> by Catherine LePage</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Lepage depicts her experiences with anxiety through wonderfully—and sometimes hilariously—accurate illustrations, like a seal balancing a bomb on its nose and a porcupine traversing a room full of balloons. If that doesn&#8217;t represent how anxiety sometimes feels, I don&#8217;t know what does. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/when-anxiety-attacks.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/076792083X/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=076792083X\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"When Panic Attacks: The New, Drug-Free Anxiety Therapy That Can Change Your Life\" data-publisher=\"Harmony\" data-releasedate=\"2007-06-12\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">When Anxiety Attacks</a></em> by Terian Koscik</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>This illustrated memoir recounts Koscik&#8217;s experiences with anxiety and how finally deciding to go to therapy changed her life. Full of honesty and humor, and I&#8217;m all for helping people see the immense value of therapy and getting help for mental health issues. Do it, do it, do it. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/its-all-absolutely-fine.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/144948042X/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=144948042X\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"It's All Absolutely Fine: Life Is Complicated So I've Drawn It Instead\" data-publisher=\"Andrews McMeel Publishing\" data-releasedate=\"2017-01-31\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">It&#8217;s All Absolutely Fine</a></em> by Ruby Elliot</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>The daily struggles of life with mental illness are brought to life with care and hilarity in these comics from the creator of Rubyetc. Elliot brings her signature wry sense of humor, making this serious topic fun to read about. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"5 Books To Get Your Buddhism Through Poetry","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=442944","description":"\n<p>According to Dictionary.com, Buddhism is “a religion […] holding that life is full of suffering caused by desire and that the way to end this suffering is through enlightenment that enables one to halt the endless sequence of births and deaths to which one is otherwise subject.” That’s a whole lot to take in. I like to think of Buddhism as a conscious way of life. It’s a school of thought that focuses on working towards and being grateful for an inner peace. It allows us to get in touch with who we actually are at our core. Maybe this is a bit difficult to follow, too. <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/books-about-buddhism/\">The last time I wrote about Buddhism, I offered books that may explain all this in greater detail</a>. Additionally, Buddhist writings lend themselves to poetry. They share pretty language and decorated verse. Check out these Buddhist-inspired works to explore your own Buddhism while getting your poetry on. </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00KGZT60E/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B00KGZT60E\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/A-Full-Load-of-Moonlight-Chinese-Chan-Buddhist-Poems-1.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00KGZT60E/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B00KGZT60E\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"A Full Load of Moonlight: Chinese Chan Buddhist Poems\" data-publisher=\"Musical Stone Culture\" data-releasedate=\"2014-05-20\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">A Full Load of Moonlight</a>: Chinese Chan Buddhist Poems by Mary M.Y. Fung (Translator) and David Lunde (Translator)</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>This book of translations offers poems from Chan monastics and lay people. The poems in both sections date back to the early 600s CE. They run through the centuries up to the more recent 1800s (that doesn’t seem recent, but in comparison to three-digit-years, it’s closer to today). Chan Buddhism has a Chinese foundation; the introduction explains simply, “Chan is a state of mind and a way of life.” If you typically skip introductions, do your best to not skip this one. It explains pretty simply the background of Chan Buddhism, upon which these 180 poems are based. Another neat feature of this collection is that the original poems (in Chinese characters) appear above the translations. A lot of the poems have themes of the natural world, and that’s because a lot of Buddhism reflects the natural world, which includes the world of the mind. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1570625506/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1570625506\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Songs-of-Spiritual-Experience-Tibetan-Buddhist-Poems-of-Insight-and-Awakening.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1570625506/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1570625506\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Songs of Spiritual Experience: Tibetan Buddhist Poems of Insight and Awakening\" data-publisher=\"Shambhala\" data-releasedate=\"2000-12-19\" class=\"butter\">Songs of Spiritual Experience: Tibetan Buddhist Poems of Insight and Awakening</a> by Thupten Jinpa and Jas Elsner</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>This collection presents poems from the 11th Century through today. These 52 poems are broken down into thematic sections, so you can find a theme that strikes you rather than follow a chronology. You can choose from the transience of life, solitude, finding a guru, emptiness, awakenings, and mystic visions. There’s also a section of poems that focus on the life of the poets in a Buddhist, reflective way. To help along with understanding the philosophies in the verses, there are several introductions, a glossary, and notes. Basically, this book can act as a class in Tibetan Buddhism and poetry all at once. Plus, the poems are pretty. That’s always a plus. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/161180776X/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=161180776X\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/The-First-Free-Women-Poems-of-the-Early-Buddhist-Nuns.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/161180776X/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=161180776X\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"The First Free Women: Poems of the Early Buddhist Nuns\" data-publisher=\"Shambhala\" data-releasedate=\"2020-02-11\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The First Free Women: Poems of the Early Buddhist Nuns</a> by Matty Weingast and Bhikkhuni Anandabodhi (Foreword)</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>I find this collection fascinating—it’s poems by the first Buddhist nuns, the first official female practitioners of Buddhism. These poems, Versus of the Elder Nuns, or the <em>Therigatha</em>, portray the life and emotions of these women with a Buddhist reflection. Though some poems are unfinished, they all offer insight into the beginnings of a school of belief from incredibly unique points of view. There is struggle, and there is love. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1949039056/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1949039056\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/The-World-I-Leave-You-Asian-American-Poets-on-Faith-and-Spirit.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1949039056/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1949039056\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"The World I Leave You: Asian American Poets on Faith &#38; Spirit\" data-publisher=\"Orison Books\" data-releasedate=\"2020-05-05\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The World I Leave You: Asian American Poets on Faith &#38; Spirit</a> by Leah Silvieus (Editor) and Lee Herrick (Editor)</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>The poems in this collection are not all about Buddhism. Some are, while others venture into different religions and beliefs. These poets of the Asian diaspora present their own faiths and personal experiences through verse. If your way to Buddhism is to explore a variety of wisdoms in a more contemporary framework, you may want to start here. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Call-Me-By-My-True-Names-The-Collected-Poems-of-Thich-Nhat-Hanh.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" aria-hidden=\"true\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1888375167/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1888375167\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Call Me By My True Names: The Collected Poems of Thich Nhat Hanh\" data-publisher=\"Parallax Press\" data-releasedate=\"2001-08-09\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Call Me By My True Names: The Collected Poems of Thich Nhat Hanh</a></h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Thich Nhat Hanh is a Buddhist monk, and his writings are widely known. Through poetry and prose, he clearly and simply offers wisdom. Really, any description I write here can’t quite explain how his clarity and simplicity offer more than any high-falutin’ explanations of Buddhism. Read the poems, and you’ll see what I mean. </p></div></div></div>\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<p>Poetry is a natural way into Buddhism. The texts speak to each other in a way that prose may not be able to. If you want to explore more, <a href=\"https://bookriot.com/books-about-buddhism/\">you can read the books listed here</a>. Much gratitude for reading. </p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:qj6IDK7rITs\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=qj6IDK7rITs\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:I9og5sOYxJI\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=I9og5sOYxJI\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:oK5efhrsFR0\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?i=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:oK5efhrsFR0\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:gIN9vFwOqvQ\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?i=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:gIN9vFwOqvQ\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:ZC7T4KBF6Nw\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=ZC7T4KBF6Nw\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=Tc1HBoFApGw:aY8Lxlqmx3Y:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=yIl2AUoC8zA\" border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/bookriot/WlRy/~4/Tc1HBoFApGw\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 28 Aug 2020 10:38:00 +0000","feedId":9916,"bgimg":"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image-of-golden-buddha-statue.jpg.optimal.jpg","linkMd5":"6d0b66854b64d37dcb15f95ce04349e6","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn21@2020_5/2020/08/31/08-19-42-272_db23e36f14a661f8.webp","destWidth":700,"destHeight":375,"sourceBytes":82691,"destBytes":78578,"author":"Christina M. She returns to her family home in Caddo Lake, Texas, hoping to vanquish the demons of her past. than darkness! On one hand, the word gothic embodies everything macabre about humanity. Indeed, orators expressing a darker theme stands alongside light-hearted topics! On the other, darkness is multilayered. Writing is truly a companion to everyone&#8217;s life. </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GothicPoems1.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Gothic Poems. A lantern glows in the night sky. A tree sits on the left. File name: GothicPoems1.jpg\" class=\"wp-image-443774\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GothicPoems1.jpg.optimal.jpg 600w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GothicPoems1-300x171.jpg.optimal.jpg 300w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GothicPoems1-50x29.jpg.optimal.jpg 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" /><figcaption><span>Photo by <a href=\"https://unsplash.com/@kerber?utm_source=unsplash&#38;utm_medium=referral&#38;utm_content=creditCopyText\">Marko Blažević</a> on <a href=\"https://unsplash.com/s/photos/gothic?utm_source=unsplash&#38;utm_medium=referral&#38;utm_content=creditCopyText\">Unsplash</a></span></figcaption></figure></div>\n<h3>Gothic Poetry&#8217;s Roots</h3>\n<p>During the 19th century, Edgar Allen Poe gave gothic poetry a voice. Pieces such as &#8220;Annabel Lee&#8221; and &#8220;The Raven&#8221; conveys loss and heartbreak. His sadness speaks to many who searches for kindred spirits to listen. Christina Rossetti was another poet with gothic roots. Her piece &#8220;Goblin Market&#8221; is well renowned, warnings of goblin men creeping in orchards on summer days.  </p>\n<h3>Gothic Poems: Expressive and Emotional</h3>\n<p>As time moved on, the definition of gothic broadened. For example, the term specifically defines a <a href=\"https://www.tor.com/2012/06/19/whats-gothic-now/\">foreboding of bad omens</a>. This could describe either a paranormal experience or a traumatic event in life. Poets express somber times in a variety of instances. Despite its horror origins, gothic poems reflect both an appreciation of the eccentric and a yearning for acceptance. </p>\n<h2>16 Gothic Poems From Talented Artists</h2>\n<p>This group features poets unashamed of their dark side! These artists use music and spoken word to share their unique outlook on life. Despite their departure of sunny passages, their words represent power. </p>\n<h3>Rios de la Luz: &#8220;Itza&#8221;</h3>\n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed-youtube aligncenter wp-block-embed 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"Books With Hilarious Titles (That Are Very Serious In Context)","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=442986","description":"\n<p>Sometimes you know you shouldn&#8217;t laugh, but you do it anyway. Sometimes you <em>don&#8217;t</em> know you shouldn&#8217;t laugh, and are then embarrassed when you do because you look like a dope. I present to you this list of hilarious titles about serious topics, in honor of one particularly choice incident when I laughed at a colleague who wanted a book about extraterrestrial invaders, only to discover that it was actually a well-reputed counter-insurgency thought experiment. Live and learn! Join me in embarrassed laughter, won&#8217;t you?</p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1439134421/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1439134421\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Alien-Invasion-How-to-Defend-the-Earth.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Alien Invasion: How to Defend the Earth\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1439134421/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1439134421\" target=\"_blank\">Alien Invasion: How to Defend the Earth</a> by Travis Taylor and Bob Boan </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>This is the first of many hilarious titles that embarrassed the heck out of me when it turned out to be serious! Imagine, if you  dare, a technologically superior enemy with inscrutable aims that  descends on your home with laser guns a-blazin&#8217;. Would you a) waste your  life and energy in a noble but ultimately futile direct attack; b) try  to get out of the way and end up a refugee; or c) pretend to submit in  order to learn about your enemy and steal their stuff for the  Resistance? The more you think about it, the more interesting it gets. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1594745250/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1594745250\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Crafting-with-Cat-Hair.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Crafting with Cat Hair\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"Crafting with Cat Hair (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1594745250/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1594745250\" target=\"_blank\">Crafting with Cat Hair</a> by Kaori Tsutaya, Translated by  Amy Hirschman  </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p> Crafting your cat into finger puppets! Yay! If you just shot a bunch of  water out of your nose over this title, you&#8217;re not alone. I, too, find  this concept extremely risible. However, this book is <em>actually</em> an easy introduction to felting, and felting is serious stuff. The  artwork you create with it can be incredibly realistic, detailed, and versatile. It also takes a <em>ton</em> of expensive materials—think  buckets and buckets of animal fiber—and patience. If your cat is willing to contribute at least one of those things, you&#8217;re probably  going to have a better experience. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0875Z8543/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B0875Z8543\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Everybody-Poops.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Everyone Poops\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0875Z8543/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B0875Z8543\">Everyone Poops</a> by Taro Gomi </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>If you want to break into full-throated REM every single time you see this book, then welcome to the club! (<em>Ev&#8217;ry-body poooooooooops…some-times…)</em> That said, you <em>have</em> probably heard of this book. It&#8217;s a great way to talk about one of  those implacable facts of life with your young kids in a way that  doesn&#8217;t shame them. Obviously, it&#8217;s meant for toileting years, and  anything that makes those easier is absolutely a serious and valuable  piece of work. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0674025555/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0674025555\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Are-Women-Human.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Are Women Human?\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0674025555/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0674025555\" target=\"_blank\">Are Women Human?</a> by Catharine A. MacKinnon </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>At first glance, this falls into the category of hilarious titles that are just trying to get your attention. At second, you realize a woman wrote it and think it&#8217;ll be a sly wink at sexism. Then you open it and  it gets right into the genocide, slavery, and systematic rape. This is  the kind of book that asks a ridiculous question—do women worldwide enjoy full human status?—and then breaks it down until you realize that it&#8217;s not even remotely a silly question. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Is-Eating-People-Wrong.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Is eating people wrong\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"> <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0521188512/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0521188512\" target=\"_blank\">Is Eating People Wrong?</a> by Allan C. Hutchinson </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>A book for the Hannibal fans amongst us! Before you slide into <em>if eating people is wrong, I don&#8217;t want to be right</em>, consider the question in a legal light. That&#8217;s what this book does! With wit and humor, it relates the stories that shaped some of  what we think of as basic morality, but which are actually more about  law and social custom. If you&#8217;re a law student, you shouldn&#8217;t miss it. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1509526404/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1509526404\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Race-After-Technology.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Race After Technology\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1509526404/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1509526404\" target=\"_blank\">Race After Technology</a> by Ruha Benjamin </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>This title is here because the syntax suggests a bizarre physical pursuit of an ever-evasive flying iPhone. However, it&#8217;s actually about how technology changes and exacerbates racial injustice, and it is a heckin&#8217; important read for our modern era. Benjamin introduces the concept of &#8220;The New Jim Code&#8221; and provides some very valuable tools for  breaking down a new, insidious form of racism. </p></div></div></div>\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<p><em>But wait! 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"Everything We Know So Far About Diana Gabaldon’s New Outlander Book: GO TELL THE BEES THAT I AM GONE","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=443315","description":"\n<p>So, you&#8217;ve read all of the Outlander books and the Lord John spin-offs, you&#8217;re caught up on the TV show, and you&#8217;re waiting as patiently as you know how for book 9, <em>Go Tell The Bees That I Am Gone</em>. You have consumed literally countless hours and hundreds of thousands of words in the world of the Scottish Highlands and a young United States of America. Well, fellow fan of Scottish time travel fiction, there&#8217;s good news and kinda good news when it comes to the new Outlander<em> </em>book. As far as I can tell, however, there is no actually <em>bad</em> news. Which is good! Let&#8217;s continue. </p>\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0385319959/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0385319959\" target=\"_blank\"><em>Outlander</em></a> was first published in 1991, which is incidentally the year the George R.R. Martin started writing <em>A Game of Thrones </em>(published 1996)<em>.</em> Since then, Diana Gabaldon&#8217;s series has grown to eight core novels of a planned ten. The side series of historical mysteries about everyone&#8217;s favorite secondary character, Lord John Grey, includes three novels and six novellas. Other short stories and novellas have been published in various collections over the years, including one about Roger&#8217;s parents during WWII, and another about how Ian Murray Sr. and Jamie Fraser became mercenaries as teens. There is a graphic novel, a two-volume companion guide, and—of course—a television show. </p>\n<p>Before we move on, please take a moment to appreciate the 1991 first edition cover of <em>Outlander</em>: </p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Outlander-1991_1st_Edition_cover.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-443555\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Outlander-1991_1st_Edition_cover.jpg.optimal.jpg 255w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Outlander-1991_1st_Edition_cover-197x300.jpg.optimal.jpg 197w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Outlander-1991_1st_Edition_cover-246x375.jpg.optimal.jpg 246w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Outlander-1991_1st_Edition_cover-33x50.jpg.optimal.jpg 33w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 255px) 100vw, 255px\" /><figcaption>I love it so much for being of its time. </figcaption></figure></div>\n<p>Book 8 of the series, <em>Written in my Own Heart&#8217;s Blood</em>, was published in 2014. Since then, Diana Gabaldon has been working on book 9, <em>Go Tell the Bees That I Am Gone</em>. The good news is that Gabaldon said on Facebook in August 16 that the manuscript would be done &#8220;#soon,&#8221; adding the only slightly snarky hashtags &#8220;#PatienceIsAVirtue, &#8220;NoItsNotDoneYet, and #ComingAlongNicelyThankYou.&#8221; I do appreciate an author with a sense of humor. The slightly less good news is, she said much the same thing on <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"January 15th of this year (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"http://www.dianagabaldon.com/2020/01/amazon-is-wrong-no-bees-publication-date-yet/\" target=\"_blank\">January 15 of this year</a>. At that point, the publication date of Oct 20 was erroneously published on Amazon and affiliate sites. Gabaldon posted in her blog that there was no way the publication date could be set because the manuscript was not yet done, and assured her readers that the moment publication was confirmed, she would tell us.  Without drawing too many comparisons <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"to other books (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://bookriot.com/the-winds-of-winter-release-date/\" target=\"_blank\">to other books</a> we <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"may or may not still be waiting for (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://twitter.com/GRRM/status/1288539988724981761?s=20\" target=\"_blank\">may or may not still be waiting for</a>, I do trust Gabaldon that she&#8217;s actually working on the book and making progress because she posts small excerpts of her work regularly. </p>\n<p>And that&#8217;s the actual best news I have for you today: Diana Gabaldon has clearly been working diligently on book 9 despite the roadblock of 2020 in her path. </p>\n<h2>What will the new Outlander book be about?</h2>\n<p><em>SPOILERS FOR WRITTEN IN MY OWN HEART&#8217;S BLOOD AHEAD; if you haven&#8217;t read it, skip the following paragraph and rejoin us on the other side.</em></p>\n<p>When we last left Jamie and Claire, they were in North Carolina at Fraser&#8217;s Ridge. Claire was wounded at the Battle of Monmouth (insert <em>Hamilton</em> reference here); Fergus&#8217;s print shop had burned down—taking his small son Henri-Christian with it—and some time travel stuff happened that I can&#8217;t quite recall because look, it&#8217;s been awhile. Gabaldon mentioned that several familiar characters will get their own point-of-view chapters in book 9, including Marsali and possibly Fergus. She hasn&#8217;t posted on her blog since April, but there are enough excerpts on the sidebar to whet the appetite of any fan who likes those things. I cannot confirm if anyone new has gotten a POV chapter in said excepts because I prefer going into this one unspoiled—or as unspoiled as I can be, having researched this post. </p>\n<h2>Things to Do While Waiting for <em>Go Tell The Bees That I Am Gone</em> </h2>\n<ul><li>Check out the aforementioned excerpts on <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"Diana Gabaldon's blog (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"http://www.dianagabaldon.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Diana Gabaldon&#8217;s blog</a>. As a former historian myself, I appreciate her attention to detail and explanations of the process of writing and publishing a book. </li><li>Enjoy the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"teaser trailer for Clanlands  (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.clanlandsbook.com/?fbclid=IwAR0neGW58Qd6pNaleT5UWtaXrzAC8cbTpYItCkCUamK4zvSXZey_YNKJOeA\" target=\"_blank\">teaser trailer for <em>Clanlands</em> </a>by Sam Heughan and Graham MacTavish (Jamie Fraser and Dougall Mackenzie in the Outlander TV show, for the uninitiated). </li><li>Watch the Outlander cast discuss season 5 of the show at PaleyFest 2020. </li><li>Listen to Davina Porter discuss narrating all eight (!) Outlander books to date. </li><li>And my personal favorite: read Saeed Jones&#8217;s <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"epic livetweet of Outlander season 1 (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://outlanderbts.com/outlander-s1-recap-saeed-jones-kiltdaddy/?fbclid=IwAR1CNRqYK0DjFgjgDd1GCdUvMNVLD7Hwck6UcUV2xbrbziBFmvBB5KUs6PM\" target=\"_blank\">epic livetweet of <em>Outlander</em> season 1</a>. </li></ul>\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<p>Looking to hear about new releases, regardless of whether they&#8217;re time travel or Scottish Highlander-related? to explain why roller derby appeals to queer women. A woman-centric sport? People with different body types playing a hardcore sport together? Puns? What&#8217;s not to love? Unfortunately, there have not been nearly enough books or movies to capitalize on the inherent potential of an amazing F/F roller derby romance. (I&#8217;m looking at you, <em>Whip It</em>.) I have been able to put together a list of 10 sapphic books that feature roller derby, but unfortunately, this is a very white list. There is one book on this list out in 2021 by an author of colour, but I hope that publishers seek out more roller derby stories from a variety of authors in the future, offering different points of view, because there&#8217;s no reason this list should be so white.</p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-443229\" width=\"600\" srcset=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby.jpg.optimal.jpg 800w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby-300x240.jpg.optimal.jpg 300w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby-768x614.jpg.optimal.jpg 768w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby-469x375.jpg.optimal.jpg 469w, https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Roller-Derby-50x40.jpg.optimal.jpg 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /><figcaption><a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/gt8073a/4750579595/\">&#8220;Suburbia Roller Derby Suburban Brawl at ECE &#8211; 056&#8221;</a> by <a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/gt8073a/\">gt8073a</a> is licensed under&#160;<a href=\"https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0/\">CC BY 2.0</a></figcaption></figure></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1419740792/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1419740792\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/kenzie-kickstarts-a-team-derby-daredevils.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Kenzie Kickstarts a Team\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1419740792/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1419740792\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"The Derby Daredevils: Kenzie Kickstarts a Team: (The Derby Daredevils Book #1)\" data-publisher=\"Amulet Books\" data-releasedate=\"2020-03-24\" class=\"butter\">Kenzie Kickstarts a Team</a> (The Derby Daredevils #1) by Kit Rosewater, illustrated by Sophie Escabasse  </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>One of the most exciting things I&#8217;ve seen in queer lit in the last five years or so is the emergence of LGBTQ middle grade novels! For a long time, we had picture books and YA, and nothing in between. The Derby Daredevils is a series about a junior roller derby team started by Kenzie, who is the point of view character in this first volume. Her mother is a derby girl, and she desperately wants her and her best friend to play in the new junior league, which means they have to put together a team, pronto. This is an adorable short chapter book with tons of illustrations, and a diverse cast of characters in terms of race, personality, and body types. Kenzie has a crush on a girl, and she also has a trans dad. This is a perfect pick for kids just starting to get into chapter books. (Or adults, because I loved it.)</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1534455027/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1534455027\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Bruised-by-Tanya-Boteju.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Bruised by Tanya Boteju\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1534455027/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1534455027\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Bruised\" data-publisher=\"Simon &#38; Schuster Books for Young Readers\" data-releasedate=\"2021-03-23\" class=\"butter\">Bruised</a> by Tanya Boteju (March 2021)</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Okay, I&#8217;m a little early on this, because <em>Bruised</em> doesn&#8217;t come out until 2021, but I am eagerly awaiting it. From the author of <em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1534430652/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1534430652\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Kings, Queens, and In-Betweens\" data-publisher=\"Simon Pulse\" data-releasedate=\"2019-05-07\" class=\"butter\">Kings, Queens, and In-Betweens</a></em>, this follows Daya, who is just beginning in the roller derby world. She and her parents were in an accident, and only she survived; since then, she&#8217;s been looking for ways to deal with it, usually by throwing herself into physically painful situations. She hopes that the bruises from roller derby will distract her from the emotional pain, but being part of this community ends up meaning a lot more than an excuse to throw herself into danger. I&#8217;m not sure of the exact sapphic content in this yet, but I&#8217;ve been assured that it&#8217;s there, and given her previous novel, I see no reason to doubt that!</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/On-a-Roll-Lumberjanes-Volume-9.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"On a Roll (Lumberjanes Volume 9)\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1608869571/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1608869571\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Lumberjanes Vol. 9 (9)\" data-publisher=\"BOOM! Box\" data-releasedate=\"2018-07-24\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">On a Roll</a></em> (Lumberjanes Volume 9) by Shannon Watters, Kat Leyh, Carolyn Nowak, Maarta Laiho, Aubrey Aiese, and Brooklyn Allen</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>There&#8217;s never a bad reason to read Lumberjanes, and volume 9 just happens to include a roller derby bout against some yetis. Lumberjanes has been queer from the beginning, with an adorable romance between two of the girls, and it also has trans representation in the later volumes. This volume even has a nonbinary character who starts using gender neutral pronouns and is immediately accepted! As always, this is just a fun, happy read.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1684150043/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1684150043\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/Slam-by-Pamela-Ribon.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Slam by Pamela Ribon and Veronica Fish\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1684150043/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1684150043\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"SLAM! Vol. 1 (1)\" data-publisher=\"BOOM! Box\" data-releasedate=\"2017-08-15\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Slam</a><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1684150043/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1684150043\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"SLAM! Vol. 1 (1)\" data-publisher=\"BOOM! Box\" data-releasedate=\"2017-08-15\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">!</a> by Pamela Ribon and Veronica Fish</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Jennifer and Maise meet at &#8220;Fresh Meat&#8221; orientation and immediately hit it off—unfortunately, they&#8217;re put onto different teams. As they go from being rookies to finding their places on their teams, they begin to grow apart. Does this sound like the beginning of a friends-to-rivals romance? It does. Unfortunately, this isn&#8217;t that, but we do get a lesbian character in Jennifer (who is on the cover). Part of the appeal of roller derby is the close-knit friendships and community that grow from being part of a team, and that&#8217;s what <em>Slam!</em> focuses on—so this is more about the romance of friendship! </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/51knu-ElYXL.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Roller Girl by Vanessa North\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1718953798/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1718953798\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Roller Girl (Lake Lovelace) (Volume 3)\" data-publisher=\"CreateSpace Independent Publishing Platform\" data-releasedate=\"2018-05-11\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Roller Girl</a></em> by Vanessa North</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>I might have done a romance bait-and-switch with <em>Slam!</em>, but don&#8217;t worry: most of the books on this list are proper romances. <em>Roller Girl</em> is about Tina, who is a recently divorced trans woman looking for a fresh start. When her very attractive butch plumber Joanna recommends roller derby, she jumps at the chance. The only problem is that Joanna is the coach, which means the plumber/derby girl is off limits. Will they be able to resist their mutual attraction? Will the sexual tension ever be resolved? Okay, yes, obviously. But will they be able to keep their secret relationship from the team?</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Kat-Mouse-by-Jacqueline-Heat.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Kat &#38; Mouse by Jacqueline Heat\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1733940200/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1733940200\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Kat &#38; Mouse: a Crosscannon Roller Derby romance (CRD)\" data-publisher=\"Metal Heart Press\" data-releasedate=\"2019-05-31\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Kat &#38; Mouse</a> </em>by Jacqueline Heat</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Dot Mauser is the &#8220;bad girl&#8221; of the roller derby rink. As far as she&#8217;s concerned, the referee Kat has it out for her. Little does she know that while Kat is handing Dot plenty of penalties, she has her eye on her for different reasons. During the derby&#8217;s Pride event, these two find out that they&#8217;re both artists: Dot upcycles &#8220;junk&#8221; and Kat is a photographer. They form an unlikely alliance, though Dot is sure Kat hates her. There&#8217;s plenty of drama, and some darker topics than the premise would suggest, but there&#8217;s also a lot of heat between the two characters. Bonus: this is written by a roller derby girl herself, with a preface and appendix with more information.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Crash-Into-You-by-Diana-Morland.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Crash Into You by Diana Morland\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01N9K47IL/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B01N9K47IL\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Crash Into You (Roller Derby Romance Book 1)\" data-publisher=\"LoveLight Press\" data-releasedate=\"2016-12-30\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Crash Into You</a></em> by Diana Morland</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Megan&#8217;s life revolves around roller derby, and she takes it very seriously. Yes, she&#8217;s constantly surrounded by beautiful women, but she&#8217;s never let that distract her. That is, until she finds herself falling head over heels (literally) for the opposing team&#8217;s blocker Gianna. Megan is determined to keep her focus on the competition, but it&#8217;s definitely hard to keep her eyes on the prize when she can&#8217;t stop looking at her opponent.  This is a quick, fun romance with a fat love interest and some steamy scenes. </p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/The-Real-Thing-by-Laney-Webber.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"The Real Thing by Laney Webber\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1635554780/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1635554780\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"The Real Thing\" data-publisher=\"Bold Strokes Books\" data-releasedate=\"2020-04-14\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Real Thing</a></em> by Laney Webber </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Virginia Harris is the star of a lesbian web series, and it&#8217;s gone to her head. She&#8217;s used to being recognized, and has no problem finding women. So it shouldn&#8217;t come as a surprise when she is told by Allison that she was catfished by someone using her photo. Allison seems like the perfect girl, but she&#8217;s disheartened by the whole dating app experience and is ready to jump back into roller derby before she meets Virginia—can she separate the real Virginia from the catfish version she just fell for? This is one for fans of complex and &#8220;unlikable&#8221; female characters, because Virginia is a divisive love interest.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Troll-or-Derby-by-Red-Tash.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Troll or Derby by Red Tash\"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1477583726/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1477583726\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Troll Or Derby\" data-publisher=\"CreateSpace Independent Publishing Platform\" data-releasedate=\"2012-06-14\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Troll or Derby</a></em> by Red Tash </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>And now for something completely different. Roller Deb is an outcast in her town, but when her popular sister goes missing, it&#8217;s up to her to rescue her. In her search, she finds a world of trolls, fairies, gangsters, and a bloodthirsty version of roller derby. This is a dark fantasy and includes sex, drugs, and violence. Roller Deb first is pulled into this world as part of her rescue mission, but her roller derby skills make her powerful and sought-after here, and she will have to resist being pulled under completely if she wants to escape with her sister.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Color-Jam-by-Margot-Atwell.png\" alt=\"Color Jam Roller Derby Coloring Book by Margot Atwell \"/><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><em>Color Jam Roller Derby Coloring Book</em> by Margot Atwell </h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>While I may hold roller derby&#8217;s appeal to queer women to be self-evident, Margot Atwell wrote a Huffington Post article called <a href=\"https://www.huffingtonpost.ca/entry/roller-derby-queer-women_n_5813be86e4b0390e69d05780\">Why Is Roller Derby Important To So Many Queer Women?</a> In it, she talked about why she wanted to honour queer women in her kickstarted roller derby colouring book, including how being part of the roller derby community helped her to discover her own sexuality and come out. This includes several portraits of queer roller derby role models.</p></div></div></div>\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<p>And that&#8217;s it for sapphic roller derby books I could find! Feel free to let me know (@lesbrary) if I missed any! There is also a novella in <em><a title=\"Buy from Amazon\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B081M86SZS/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=B081M86SZS\" target=\"_blank\" data-title=\"Hot Ice\" data-publisher=\"Bold Strokes Books\" data-releasedate=\"2019-12-10\" class=\"butter\">Hot Ice: 3 Romance Novellas</a></em>: “Ice on Wheels” by Aurora Rey, so there&#8217;s a bonus for you. I hope that in the coming years, we&#8217;ll see many more queer roller derby books come out, whether they&#8217;re F/F romances, nonbinary YA novels, bisexual comics, or anything else under the rainbow &#38; roller derby umbrella!</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=PTO3ya2ZCuQ:fpjhojiuHNY:qj6IDK7rITs\"><img href=\"https://www.singlecare.com/blog/news/schizophrenia-statistics/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"Over 20 million people (opens in a new tab)\">Over 20 million people</a> worldwide have schizophrenia, a mental disorder involving delusions and hallucinations that inhibit a person&#8217;s ability to think clearly. Because many people with schizophrenia start experiencing symptoms in their late teen years, YA books about schizophrenia can help those with the illness feel understood.</p>\n<p>We&#8217;ve put together seven of the best YA books about schizophrenia. Whether you have schizophrenia or want to understand more about it, these books offer strong representation for the disorder.</p>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062290118/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0062290118\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/made-you-up-by-francesca-zappia-book-cover.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Made You Up book cover\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062290118/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0062290118\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Made You Up\" data-publisher=\"Greenwillow Books\" data-releasedate=\"2017-05-02\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Made You Up</a> by Francesca Zappia</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>As someone with paranoid schizophrenia, Alex has a difficult time determining what is or isn&#8217;t real around her. Through supports like her little sister and items like her Magic 8-Ball, she hopes to keep her symptoms at bay long enough to make it into college. When Alex meets Miles on her first day of classes, she&#8217;s not sure if she imagined him or not. But as Alex begins to make friends and fall in love for the first time in her life, she struggles to adjust to her &#8220;new normal&#8221; after a lifetime coping with mental illness.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a product-id=\"1481422251\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1481422251/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1481422251\" target=\"_blank\" butter=\"butter\" nofollow=\"nofollow\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"The Place Between Breaths\" data-publisher=\"Atheneum/Caitlyn Dlouhy Books\" data-releasedate=\"2018-03-27\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">The Place Between Breaths</a> by An Na</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Grace lost her mother to schizophrenia after her delusions made her believe that the only way to keep her family safe was to run away. To cope with her grief, she works as a recruiter for a local lab that hopes to find a cure for schizophrenia. But when Grace develops symptoms of the illness, she struggles to determine what is real and what may be the beginning of psychosis.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a product-id=\"0545474337\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0545474337/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0545474337\" target=\"_blank\" butter=\"butter\" nofollow=\"nofollow\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"The Memory of Light\" data-publisher=\"Arthur A. Stork</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>After a suicide attempt, 16-year-old Vicky Cruz finds herself in the mental disorders ward of Lakeview Hospital. Here she meets people who, like her, are struggling to cope with the world around them—including Gabriel, a fellow patient who has religious schizophrenic delusions.
