Ever since her dad left, Aura has taken care of her mother. </p><p>But as her mother&#8217;s condition worsens, the only way Aura can cope is through art. As Aura desperately tries to turn her pain into something beautiful, she discovers that even in her darkest hour, love and family can still be a light.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a product-id=\"0061134147\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0061134147/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0061134147\" target=\"_blank\" butter=\"butter\" nofollow=\"nofollow\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Challenger Deep\" data-publisher=\"Quill Tree Books\" data-releasedate=\"2016-04-26\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Challenger Deep</a> by Neal Schusterman</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Caden Bosh believes he is on a ship headed for the Mariana Trench: a perilous mission where he could easily lose his life. But in the real world, he&#8217;s a high school student who&#8217;s slowly succumbing to hallucinations that are hard to dismiss. When he discovers the truth behind his psychosis, he struggles to gain control of his mind.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a product-id=\"0147508851\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0147508851/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0147508851\" target=\"_blank\" butter=\"butter\" nofollow=\"nofollow\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Schizo: A novel\" data-publisher=\"Speak\" data-releasedate=\"2015-09-08\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Schizo</a> by Nick Scheff</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Miles would do anything to find his younger brother Teddy, who went missing without a trace. But the closer he thinks he gets to finding Teddy, the further away he seems. As Miles descends into psychosis, he must come to terms with both his schizophrenia and the loss of his brother.</p></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"wp-block-book-blurb-block-main bookblurb-block\"><div class=\"card__content\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1250104254/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1250104254\"><img class=\"bookblurb__image\" src=\"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/51hJtbTMBfL.jpg.optimal.jpg\" alt=\"Calvin cover\"/></a><h3 class=\"bookblurb__booktitle\"><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1250104254/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=1250104254\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" data-title=\"Calvin: A Novel\" data-publisher=\"Square Fish\" data-releasedate=\"2017-03-21\" class=\"butter\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Calvin</a> by Martine Leavitt</h3><div class=\"bookblurb__description\"><p>Calvin was born on the day the last Calvin and Hobbes strip was published. The comic strip meant everything to him growing up and, as a teenager, his schizophrenic delusions involve a familiar-looking tiger. Soon, Calvin begins to believe that Bill Watterson—the artist behind Calvin and Hobbes—is the key to curing his illness. 16:19:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 16:19:41","title":"From Mythic Maps to 1001 Nights: 9 of Twitter’s Delightful Lit Bots","link":"https://bookriot.com/?p=434930","description":"<p>There are a lot of bots. In 2018, <a href=\"https://www.vox.com/technology/2018/4/9/17214720/pew-study-bots-generate-two-thirds-of-twitter-links\">a study estimated</a> that bots post around 2/3rds of the links on Twitter. In 2019, a study suggested bots are <a href=\"https://www.defenseone.com/technology/2019/09/twitter-bots-are-becoming-more-human-study/159697/\">acting more human</a>. This May, a study found that <a href=\"https://www.npr.org/sections/coronavirus-live-updates/2020/05/20/859814085/researchers-nearly-half-of-accounts-tweeting-about-coronavirus-are-likely-bots\">nearly half the accounts tweeting</a> about COVID-19 are probably bots.</p>\n<p>Most bots are banal. Some bots are malicious. But there are also a few bots that bring a bit of wonder and poetry into your timeline.</p>\n<h3>1. Sappho Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/sapphobot\">@sapphobot</a></h3>\n<p>If you&#8217;re a fan of fragments of lyric Greek poetry, this is a bot for you. The Sappho Bot posts fragments of translations from Anne Carson&#8217;s <em><a class=\"butter\" title=\"Buy from Amazon\" href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0375724516/ref=as_li_tf_il?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=boorio-20&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;camp=217145&#38;creative=399349&#38;creativeASIN=0375724516\" rel=\"nofollow\">If Not, Winter: Fragments of Sappho </a></em> and more. Some modifications have been made to fit the character limit.</p>\n<p>Recent poem-fragments include:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">farewell</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">     bride</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">        farewell</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">            much-honored bridegroom</p>\n<p>and:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">bittersweet, undefeated creature</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">– against you there is no defence</p>\n<h3>2. Anne Carson Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/carsonbot\">@carsonbot</a></h3>\n<p>Speaking of Anne Carson, there&#8217;s also a bot that tweets Anne Carson quotes every two hours.</p>\n<p>Carson (b. 1950) is a poet, essayist, professor of Classics, and translator. Recent tweets include:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Sometimes I think language should cover its own eyes when it speaks.</p>\n<p>And:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Winter exists and winter is never soon enough.</p>\n<h3>3. Sylvia Plath Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/SylviaPlathBot\">@SylviaPlathBot</a></h3>\n<p>The Plath bot tweets random bits of Sylvia Plath&#8217;s poetry every hour. Plath (1932–1963) is best known for her confessional poetry and her semi-autobiographical novel, <em>The Bell Jar.</em></p>\n<p>For instance:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">I am not a tree with my root in the soil</p>\n<p>and:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Above the appalling ruin; in bleak light</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Of your stormy eye, magic takes flight</p>\n<h3>4. Emily Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/BotDickinson\">@BotDickinson</a></h3>\n<p>What would Twitter be without an Emily Bot? Poems from the great Emily Dickinson (1830–1886) fit particularly well with Twitter&#8217;s character count. To whit:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">I&#8217;m Nobody! Who are you?</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Are you &#8211; Nobody &#8211; too?</p>\n<h3>5. Nights Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/the_small_hours\">@the_small_hours</a></h3>\n<p>The Nights Bot is my all-time favorite, and the one I find myself talking to the most. This bot features fragments from Yasmine Seale&#8217;s forthcoming translation of the <em>1001 Nights. </em>Seale is not only an accomplished poet and translator but the first woman to translate this important world classic to English.</p>\n<p>The snippets are almost all wonderfully short. They include:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">a ruin for the owls and crows to haunt</p>\n<p>And:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">perfumed herself, took my sword and left</p>\n<p>(I can&#8217;t wait for Yasmine&#8217;s translation to be out.)</p>\n<h3>6. Magical Realism Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/MagicRealismBot\">@MagicalRealismBot</a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"css-901oao css-16my406 r-1qd0xha r-ad9z0x r-bcqeeo r-qvutc0\">The Magical Realism Bot is predictably unpredictable. Constructed by @chrisrodley and @yeldora, it generates a magical story every four hours. </span></p>\n<p>It will tell you, for instance, that:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">In Budapest there is a book that is made of HR managers.</p>\n<p>And:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">A screenwriter plays a game of rock, paper, scissors with a woolly mammoth.</p>\n<p>Could happen.</p>\n<h3>7. Queer Lit Bot <a href=\"https://twitter.com/queerlitbot\">@QueerLitBot</a></h3>\n<p>This bot tweets queer poetry, prose, and plays. They try to maintain formatting whenever possible and promise that &#8220;extracts tend to be hopeful.&#8221;</p>\n<p>From a recent tweet:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">And I knew when I entered her</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">I was high wind in her forest’s hollow</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">fingers whispering sound</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">honey flowed</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Audre Lorde, Love Poem</p>\n<p>And:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">When you came, you were like red wine and honey</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">And the taste of you burnt my mouth with its sweetness</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Amy Lowell, Decade</p>\n<h3>8. Mythic Maps <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mythicmaps\">@MythicMaps</a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"css-901oao css-16my406 r-1qd0xha r-ad9z0x r-bcqeeo r-qvutc0\">Mythic Maps is a bot by @mewo2 that offers maps from fantasy and science fiction novels.</span></p>\n<p>You&#8217;ll find a map of The Free Cities from <em>A Dance with Dragons</em> by George R.R. Martin alongside a map from <em>The Witches of Wenshar</em> by Barbara Hambly—and more.</p>\n<h3>9. Moby-Dick <a href=\"https://twitter.com/MobyDickatSea\">@MobyDickatSea</a></h3>\n<p>Moby-Dick was my first twitter bot, and it remains an inspiration. The bot provides more than 2,000 lines handpicked from <em>Moby-Dick</em>, one at a time in random order.</p>\n<p>The lines are often rich in sonic resonance, as:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Alike, joy and sorrow, hope and fear, seemed ground to finest dust, and powdered, for the time, in the clamped mortar of Ahab&#8217;s iron soul.</p>\n<p>Sometimes wonderfully pithy, and easy to apply to any moment in one&#8217;s life:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">don’t you know the higher you climb, the colder it gets?</p>\n<p>And often full of Herman Melville&#8217;s characteristic wit:</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">Surely his was a touch of fine philosophy; though no doubt he had never heard there was such a thing as that.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:qj6IDK7rITs\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=qj6IDK7rITs\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:I9og5sOYxJI\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=I9og5sOYxJI\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:oK5efhrsFR0\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?i=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:oK5efhrsFR0\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:gIN9vFwOqvQ\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?i=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:gIN9vFwOqvQ\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:ZC7T4KBF6Nw\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=ZC7T4KBF6Nw\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?a=BWz_W5MVdX0:cip1AbaO0VY:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/bookriot/WlRy?d=yIl2AUoC8zA\" border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/bookriot/WlRy/~4/BWz_W5MVdX0\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 28 Aug 2020 10:37:54 +0000","feedId":9916,"bgimg":"https://s2982.pcdn.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image-of-neon-wall-sign-reading-tweettweet.jpg.optimal.jpg","linkMd5":"58bc6678d53c7afff901eec792248d6b","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn40@2020_5/2020/08/31/08-19-41-779_292cf8a522db70b3.webp","destWidth":700,"destHeight":384,"sourceBytes":78773,"destBytes":71074,"author":"M.
